cb_check_queue_attributes = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			num_queued_constructions <= 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_queue_size
			value = 0
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			num_queued_constructions > 50
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_queue_size
			value = 50
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_queue_size
			value = num_queued_constructions
		}
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = cb_queue_size
		multiply = construction_cost_medium
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = cb_queue_size
		divide = 15
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = cb_queue_size
		subtract = modifier:country_construction_add
	}
}

cb_construction_points_target = {
	set_variable = {
		name = PSR_input
		value = var:incorporated_population
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = PSR_input
		divide = 1000000
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = PSR_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:PSR_input >= 25
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_root
			value = 5.0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_square
			value = 25.0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_delta
			value = var:PSR_square
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = PSR_delta
			subtract = var:PSR_input
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				var:PSR_delta < 0
				var:PSR_root < 100
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = PSR_root
				add = 0.1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_square
				value = var:PSR_root
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = PSR_square
				multiply = var:PSR_root
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_delta
				value = var:PSR_square
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = PSR_delta
				subtract = var:PSR_input
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_output
			value = var:PSR_root
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_output
			value = var:PSR_input
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = PSR_output
			divide = 5
		}
	}
	
	set_variable = {
		name = GSR_input
		value = gdp
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = GSR_input
		divide = 1000000
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = GSR_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:GSR_input >= 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_root
			value = 1.0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_square
			value = 1.0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_delta
			value = var:GSR_square
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = GSR_delta
			subtract = var:GSR_input
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				var:GSR_delta < 0
				var:GSR_root < 100
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = GSR_root
				add = 0.1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_square
				value = var:GSR_root
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = GSR_square
				multiply = var:GSR_root
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_delta
				value = var:GSR_square
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = GSR_delta
				subtract = var:GSR_input
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:GSR_delta < 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_output
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_output
				value = var:GSR_root
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_output
			value = var:GSR_input
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = GSR_output
			divide = 1
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:PSR_output >= 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:PSR_output > GSR_output
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_output
				value = var:GSR_output
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = PSR_output
			multiply = 30
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = GSR_output
			multiply = 10
		}
		
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_construction_points_profitable
			value = var:PSR_output
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = cb_construction_points_profitable
			add = var:GSR_output
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:PSR_output > GSR_output
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_output
				value = var:GSR_output
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = PSR_output
			multiply = 40
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_construction_points_profitable
			value = var:PSR_output
		}
	}
	
	remove_variable = PSR_input
	remove_variable = PSR_root
	remove_variable = PSR_square
	remove_variable = PSR_delta
	remove_variable = PSR_output
	remove_variable = GSR_input
	remove_variable = GSR_root
	remove_variable = GSR_square
	remove_variable = GSR_delta
	remove_variable = GSR_output
}

cb_bureaucracy_target = {
	set_variable = {
		name = cb_bureaucracy_incorporation
		value = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				is_incorporated = no
				incorporation_progress <= 0
			}
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = no
				incorporation_progress <= 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root.var:cb_bureaucracy_incorporation < state_population
				}
				root = {
					set_variable = {
						name = cb_bureaucracy_incorporation
						value = prev.state_population
					}
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = cb_bureaucracy_incorporation
			divide = 10000
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:cb_bureaucracy_incorporation > institution_bureaucracy_cost
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_bureaucracy_important
			value = var:cb_bureaucracy_incorporation
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_bureaucracy_important
			value = institution_bureaucracy_cost
		}
	}
	remove_variable = cb_bureaucracy_incorporation
}

cb_convoys_target = {
	set_variable = {
		name = PSR_input
		value = var:incorporated_population
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = PSR_input
		divide = 1000000
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = PSR_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:PSR_input >= 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_root
			value = 0.1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_square
			value = 0.01
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_delta
			value = var:PSR_square
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = PSR_delta
			subtract = var:PSR_input
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				var:PSR_delta < 0
				var:PSR_root < 100
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = PSR_root
				add = 0.1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_square
				value = var:PSR_root
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = PSR_square
				multiply = var:PSR_root
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_delta
				value = var:PSR_square
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = PSR_delta
				subtract = var:PSR_input
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:PSR_delta < 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_output
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = PSR_output
				value = var:PSR_root
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = PSR_output
			value = var:PSR_input
		}
	}
	
	set_variable = {
		name = GSR_input
		value = gdp
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = GSR_input
		divide = 1000000
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = GSR_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:GSR_input >= 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_root
			value = 0.1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_square
			value = 0.01
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_delta
			value = var:GSR_square
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = GSR_delta
			subtract = var:GSR_input
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				var:GSR_delta < 0
				var:GSR_root < 100
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = GSR_root
				add = 0.1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_square
				value = var:GSR_root
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = GSR_square
				multiply = var:GSR_root
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_delta
				value = var:GSR_square
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = GSR_delta
				subtract = var:GSR_input
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:GSR_delta < 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_output
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = GSR_output
				value = var:GSR_root
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = GSR_output
			value = var:GSR_input
		}
	}
	
	change_variable = {
		name = PSR_output
		multiply = 600
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = GSR_output
		multiply = 300
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:PSR_output > GSR_output
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_convoys_profitable
			value = var:GSR_output
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = cb_convoys_profitable
			value = var:PSR_output
		}
	}
	
	remove_variable = PSR_input
	remove_variable = PSR_root
	remove_variable = PSR_square
	remove_variable = PSR_delta
	remove_variable = PSR_output
	remove_variable = GSR_input
	remove_variable = GSR_root
	remove_variable = GSR_square
	remove_variable = GSR_delta
	remove_variable = GSR_output
}

cb_building_limits = {
	set_variable = {
		name = CSR_input
		value = modifier:country_construction_add
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = CSR_input
		nearest = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:CSR_input >= 9
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = CSR_root
			value = 3.0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = CSR_square
			value = 9.0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = CSR_delta
			value = var:CSR_square
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = CSR_delta
			subtract = var:CSR_input
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				var:CSR_delta < 0
				var:CSR_root < 100
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = CSR_root
				add = 0.5
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = CSR_square
				value = var:CSR_root
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = CSR_square
				multiply = var:CSR_root
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = CSR_delta
				value = var:CSR_square
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = CSR_delta
				subtract = var:CSR_input
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = CSR_output
			value = var:CSR_root
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = CSR_output
			value = 3.0
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = cb_building_limit
		value = var:CSR_output
	}
	
	remove_variable = CSR_input
	remove_variable = CSR_root
	remove_variable = CSR_square
	remove_variable = CSR_delta
	remove_variable = CSR_output
}

cb_check_arable_resources = {
	state_region = {
		remove_variable = bg_coffee_plantations remove_variable = bg_tea_plantations remove_variable = bg_dye_plantations remove_variable = bg_tobacco_plantations remove_variable = bg_opium_plantations remove_variable = bg_sugar_plantations remove_variable = bg_banana_plantations remove_variable = bg_rye_farms remove_variable = bg_wheat_farms remove_variable = bg_rice_farms remove_variable = bg_maize_farms remove_variable = bg_millet_farms remove_variable = bg_livestock_ranches remove_variable = bg_cotton_plantations remove_variable = bg_silk_plantations
		remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_rye_farms target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_wheat_farms target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_rice_farms target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_maize_farms target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_millet_farms target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_livestock_ranches target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_banana_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_sugar_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_cotton_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_silk_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_coffee_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_tea_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_dye_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_tobacco_plantations target = this } remove_list_global_variable = { name = bg_opium_plantations target = this } 
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_rye_farm } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_rye_farms target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_rye_farm if = { limit = { has_building = building_rye_farm } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_rye_farms target = prev } remove_building = building_rye_farm } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_wheat_farm } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_wheat_farms target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_wheat_farm if = { limit = { has_building = building_wheat_farm } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_wheat_farms target = prev } remove_building = building_wheat_farm } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }

		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_livestock_ranch } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_livestock_ranches target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_livestock_ranch if = { limit = { has_building = building_livestock_ranch } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_livestock_ranches target = prev } remove_building = building_livestock_ranch } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }

		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_coffee_plantation } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_coffee_plantations target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_coffee_plantation if = { limit = { has_building = building_coffee_plantation } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_coffee_plantations target = prev } remove_building = building_coffee_plantation } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_tea_plantation } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_tea_plantations target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_tea_plantation if = { limit = { has_building = building_tea_plantation } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_tea_plantations target = prev } remove_building = building_tea_plantation } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_dye_plantation } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_dye_plantations target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_dye_plantation if = { limit = { has_building = building_dye_plantation } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_dye_plantations target = prev } remove_building = building_dye_plantation } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_tobacco_plantation } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_tobacco_plantations target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_tobacco_plantation if = { limit = { has_building = building_tobacco_plantation } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_tobacco_plantations target = prev } remove_building = building_tobacco_plantation } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_building = building_opium_plantation } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_opium_plantations target = this } } else = { if = { limit = { NOT = { any_scope_state = { free_arable_land > 0 } } } add_arable_land = 1 set_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } random_scope_state = { limit = { free_arable_land > 0 } start_building_construction = building_opium_plantation if = { limit = { has_building = building_opium_plantation } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = bg_opium_plantations target = prev } remove_building = building_opium_plantation } } if = { limit = { has_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } add_arable_land = -1 remove_variable = cb_changed_arable_land } }
		set_variable = cb_check_arable_resources
	}
}

cb_check_special_buildings = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = colonization
			owns_treaty_port_in = STATE_SINAI
			has_variable = suez_survey_complete
			NOT = {
				s:STATE_SINAI = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_suez_canal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_SINAI = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_suez_canal
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = civilizing_mission
			owns_treaty_port_in = STATE_PANAMA
			has_variable = panama_survey_complete
			NOT = {
				s:STATE_PANAMA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_panama_canal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_PANAMA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_panama_canal
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			s:STATE_HOME_COUNTIES = {
				any_scope_state = {
					owner = root
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_big_ben
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_HOME_COUNTIES = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_big_ben
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = steel_frame_buildings
			s:STATE_ILE_DE_FRANCE = {
				any_scope_state = {
					owner = root
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_eiffel_tower
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_ILE_DE_FRANCE = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_eiffel_tower
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = steel_frame_buildings
			s:STATE_NEW_YORK = {
				any_scope_state = {
					owner = root
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_statue_of_liberty
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_NEW_YORK = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_statue_of_liberty
			}
		}
	}
}
